<p>NUVIA have the opportunity for an experienced Senior Human Factors Engineer to join us in the Defuel team at HMNB Devonport, one of the largest naval bases in Western Europe. The client is a key strategic partner to customers; the MOD and the Royal Navy. They ensure that the UK Royal Navy goes to sea safely by supporting them in Devonport and around the world. This can be worked on a hybrid\u002Fremote basis with site visits required. Please note that we can recruit on a staff or contract basis.<\u002Fp>\n <p> We are looking for individuals to support the Defuel23 programme of work, preparing a dock for defueling and dismantling of submarines.<\u002Fp>\n <p> As a Human Factors Engineer you will be involved in the preparation of Human Factors Substantiation Reports (HFSRs). This substation includes the following processes:<\u002Fp>\n <ul>\n  <li> Task Analysis<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Development of Fault Trees<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Calculation of an Initial Human Error Probability (I-HEP) using expert knowledge and experience and taking into consideration the context of the human events (e.g. Performance Shaping Factors (PSFs) and Error Producing Conditions (EPCs)).<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <p> HF input to the Verification &amp; Validation (V&amp;V) activities supporting commissioning is also part of this project. This role requires engagement with the wider safety and site teams to understand the wider project to enable the integration of Human Factors. The Defuel project is leading the way at Devonport in integrating this new process for incorporating Human Factors into the wider project, so this is an exciting opportunity to get involved.<\u002Fp>\n <p> Help us to create the naval base and dockyard of the future and in return you will receive a competitive salary, good benefits package and the unbeatable quality of life that comes with living in one of the most beautiful corners of the UK.<\u002Fp>\n <p><br> What do I need to be able to do the role?<\u002Fp>\n <p> You'll be educated to Degree level in an Engineering or Scientific discipline and\u002For have relevant knowledge and experience; a background in nuclear\u002Fradiological safety is highly beneficial for the roles we are looking to fill. <p>Nuvia are recruiting an experienced Civil Structural Engineer to work on either a staff or contract basis. Base site will be Devonport Dockyard but remote\u002Fhybrid working is available.<\u002Fp>\n <p> In order to deliver the MoD’s submarine and warship programmes, a significant programme of infrastructure investment is required on the Devonport site. The ‘Major Infrastructure Projects’ (MIP) Business Unit has been established to support this.<\u002Fp>\n <p> One of the key scope elements within MIP is establishing a defuel capability for out of service submarines, which is delivered under the programme banner of Defuel23. This work comprises of a number of interrelated projects to develop various multi-disciplinary infrastructure systems, with an overall value in excess of £100m.<\u002Fp>\n <p> The Dock Readiness project is delivering the infrastructure upgrades for the existing dry dock that will be used for the submarine defuels. The dry dock is within a nuclear licensed site. Multiple work packages form the Dock Readiness project. This role is part of that Engineering Team that is delivering the designs for each of those work packages.<\u002Fp>\n <p> The primary purpose of the role is to ultimately assist and support the Design Manager in the delivery of project scope. This will include the likes of the following;<\u002Fp>\n <ul>\n  <li> To undertake the delivery of structural engineering activities to the required scope, quality, schedule and cost.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Responsible for technical aspects of the structural engineering work packages from identification of the need, through to handover.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Undertake technical delivery of one or more design packages as directed by the Principal Civil &amp; Structural Engineer.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Ensure that the design documentation covers the scope of operations required by the Project Manager and is produced to agreed standards, schedule and budget.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Plan for effective project implementation.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Ensuring effective Quality Management Arrangements, operate and deliver through compliance with Babcock’s Business Management System and Technical Manual.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Support ensuring that the processes and activities being undertaken are appropriately documented with appropriate records maintained and configuration and quality controls applied.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Support ensuring that staff and contractors are familiar with the hazards and risks associated with the work undertaken by the delegated engineering team through effective management and communication of the Risk Assessment.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <p><br> Required Knowledge, Skills, Experience and Competences:<\u002Fp>\n <ul>\n  <li> Design of heavy civil engineering and building structures to relevant codes, preferably including seismic codes.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Knowledge of architectural design of industrial buildings.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Knowledge of building services design and installation.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Knowledge of construction techniques employed structures.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Be able to demonstrate relevant knowledge and skills required in technical design development.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Sound understanding of engineering design and safety practice as relevant to discipline, post and project requirements.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Sound understanding of Company and departmental procedures relating to Design, Health &amp; Safety and Quality requirements, and ability to manage tasks in accordance with these procedures.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Working knowledge of relevant engineering computer applications.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <p> Qualifications:<\u002Fp>\n <ul>\n  <li> The candidate will have a degree or equivalent in a Civil or Structural engineering related discipline.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Preferably working towards Chartered Engineer status and member of relevant institute.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <br> Pourquoi nous rejoindre ?\n <p><br> Nuvia is a leading international engineering, project management and services provider to the highly regulated nuclear, defence, oil &amp; gas, and science &amp; research industries. the problem solving for development of technical solutions to deficiencies or in the development of new designs.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Support the review and sentencing of new designs, methodology of for Nuclear related Works, together with all relevant Local and National Regulations and Legislation.<\u002Fli>\n  <li> Support the on-site inspection of DRDL assets for their construction, maintenance, and modification.<\u002Fli>\n <\u002Ful>\n <p><br> Qualifications and Experience Requirements:<\u002Fp>\n <ul>\n  <li> A degree in an appropriate engineering discipline.<\u002Fli>\n  <li>
